                </p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Physical characteristics and movements</span>: We collect information about or related to:</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">The position and orientation of the headset and controls to determine body pose and make your avatar’s movements more realistic.
                    </p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">The position of your headset, the speed of your controller movement, and changes in your orientation (such as when you duck while playing a game) to provide an immersive and realistic virtual experience.

                    </li><li class="">How long you’ve been physically active
                    </li><li class="">Your fitness goals and achievements
                    </li></ul></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">This allows you to track your fitness progress and helps us improve those features. For example, the sensors on Meta Quest process raw images of your surroundings and enable the headset to both process your movement and help orient you in your designated virtual reality areas. Raw images of your surroundings are processed on your device.
                  </li><li class="">Video or audio content you create and information about this content, such as the date and time you created it.
                  </li></ul></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Additionally, when you use Horizon Worlds, the last few minutes of your and other users’ most recent audio, video and other interactions in Horizon Worlds are recorded  in case you want to report anything you’ve encountered. These recordings may be stored on our servers.  We do not review these recordings unless you submit a report. If you don’t submit a report, the recordings are deleted on a rolling basis. These recordings enable you to report abuse, combat harmful conduct, and protect and support our community. Other users in close proximity to you in Horizon Worlds may submit recordings of the same event. If you submit a report, we use the attached recordings to investigate and fully resolve the report, and to help train our systems to better combat harmful behavior, after which time the recordings are deleted. In some cases, we may need to retain the recordings for longer, where it is necessary in order to comply with applicable law.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Voice interactions</span>: Voice interactions are the commands and dictations you say, including if you mistakenly invoke our voice services, as well as any background sound that happens when you use those services.                   </li><li class="">Transcripts

How do we use your information for Meta VR Products? </span></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">We use the information we collect when you use Meta VR Products for the purposes described in the <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/privacy/policy/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">Meta Privacy Policy</a> under "How do we use your information?", including (i) to provide measurement, analytics, and other promotional services (including ads and commercial content); (ii) to promote safety, security, and integrity; (iii) to communicate with you; and (iv) to research and innovate for social good.</p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">We also use the information we collect when you use Meta VR Products in the following ways:</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">To power social features and personalize and promote content</span>: We use your profile name, picture, and information about your Meta VR Product activity (including your use of Meta Quest devices and apps):
                </p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="">To send personalized commercial content
                    </li><li class="">To provide personalized content suggestions
                    </li><li class="">To display ads, offers and sponsored content in Meta VR Products
                    </li></ul></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">For example, depending on your <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="/help/quest/articles/accounts/privacy-information-and-settings/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_self">privacy settings</a>, we use information about your use of Meta Quest devices and apps to help you connect with your followers, or to encourage your followers to join you in using Meta VR Products:</p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="">To recommend products, content, and experiences to others
                    </li><li class="">To help tailor a user’s experience by helping them understand which communities or content may be most relevant to them.
                    </li></ul></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Depending on your <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="/help/quest/articles/accounts/privacy-information-and-settings/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_self">privacy settings</a>, we also use information from Meta VR Products to provide user-to-user communications and other social services across the Meta Products. This includes identifying and connecting you with your followers, or people you recently interacted with in an experience, through Meta VR Products.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">To provide and improve our Meta VR Products</span>: We use information we collect, including device performance and reliability data, to improve and develop Meta VR Products. By analyzing device performance and reliability, we can improve the hardware and software that powers your experiences with Meta VR Products. We also use your device performance and reliability information to offer and improve aspects of our services, such as voice services, hand tracking, eye tracking, Natural Facial Expressions, fit adjustment, and fitness-related experiences.
                </p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">If you use our voice services on Meta VR Products, depending on your settings, we analyze and review information about your stored voice interactions using human review and machine processes to improve, troubleshoot, and train our speech recognition systems.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">When you use the hand tracking feature in Meta Quest devices, we collect technical information, like hand tracking quality, the amount of time it takes to detect your hands, and the number of pinches you make to improve this feature and troubleshoot this feature.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">When you use the eye tracking feature in Meta Quest Pro, we collect certain data about your interactions with the feature, such as tracking quality and the amount of time it takes to detect your eyes.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">When you use the Natural Facial Expressions feature in Meta Quest expressions.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">When you use the fit adjustment  feature in Meta Quest Pro, we collect and retain data about your interactions with the feature, such as whether the setup process has been completed or how long the setup process took.</p></li></ul></li></ul><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">III. How is your information shared with others for Meta VR Products?</span></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">In addition to the sharing of information described in the Meta Privacy Policy, we share the information we collect when you use the Meta VR Products in the following ways:</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Information you make public</span>: Your Meta Horizon Profile information will be <span class="x1bvjpef">public</span> and visible to people on and off the Meta VR Products. This includes your profile name, username, picture, and avatar.
                </p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">For example, if you enter a public virtual space in Meta Quest, others can see your avatar just as they see you in a real-world public space. This means your avatar can appear in pictures, recordings, or live streams that users around you take and share. Information that you post to public areas on the Meta VR Products, such as a forum, blog, or other community tool, will also be visible to people on and off Meta VR Products, along with certain information associated with your public posts, such as the time of your post.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Third-party services &amp; applications</span>: You can interact with applications and third-party services, including content, games, apps, and other experiences, through many Meta VR Products.                       Avatar
                    </li><li class="">
                      Username
                    </li><li class="">
                      Profile name and picture
                    </li><li class="">
                      List of the people you follow and those who follow you
                    </li><li class="">
                      Your interactions with the app or third-party service, such as how long you’ve interacted with their content
                    </li><li class="">
                      Any other information you choose to share with the app or third-party service
                    </li></ul></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">If you use third-party services on Meta VR Products, the third-party services may collect information from you directly through the experiences they provide.</p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">However, you can also choose to share information with third-party services from Meta VR Products, for example:</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">You can choose to share your Meta Quest fitness and activity information with third parties to sync that information with third-party fitness services.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">If you enable eye tracking or Natural Facial Expressions in Meta Quest Pro, apps can access your abstracted gaze or abstracted facial expressions data. Please note that information you share with these (or other) third-party services will be subject to their own terms and privacy policies, not this policy.</p></li></ul></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Information that you provide when playing online</span>: When you use online multi-user apps in Meta Quest, you activity and other information you provide are visible to all within the app, including your:</p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="">
                      Avatar
                    </li><li class="">
                      In-app profile information
                    </li><li class="">
                      In-app activity
                    </li></ul></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">This information can be collected, copied, recorded, and live-streamed by other users, shared on and off Meta VR Products, and submitted to us to report abuse, combat harmful conduct, and protect and support our community. <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="/help/quest/articles/accounts/privacy-information-and-settings/reporting-someone-on-oculus/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_self">Learn more</a>. Please consider carefully who you interact with and how you conduct yourself, and make sure your available privacy settings reflect your preferences.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Third party access to voice interactions</span>: Depending on your settings, we share recordings, transcripts, and related data about your voice interactions with vendors and service providers who assist us in improving, troubleshooting, and training our speech recognition systems.</p></li></ul><div class="x16g9bbj x1p5oq8j xwxc41k xfjrbgk xw8udss xobpncf xjliv6m x1ij0wma xsp84uj x1uc5f31 xxgyeuj x166pohu xu0txxm xcxolhg xwczod1 x13mtej6 xjlskvi x1kanymm x1i6xp69 xr4g9wi x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl x1a2a7pz">Facebook View</div><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Facebook View is a wearable experience that lets you interact with your environment in new and innovative ways. The Facebook View companion app (the "App") pairs with Ray-Ban Stories glasses made and distributed by Luxottica (the "Glasses"). Meta software powers the smart features on the Glasses. This Supplemental Privacy Policy applies to "Facebook View," which means, together, the App, the software on the Glasses, and their related services and features.</p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">I. What information do we collect for Facebook View?</span></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">In addition to the information described in the Meta Privacy Policy under "<a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/privacy/policy/?section_id=1-WhatInformationDoWe" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">What information do we collect?</a>", we collect the following categories of information when you use Facebook View:</p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Photo and video information</span>: When you use the Glasses to take a photo or video, the cameras and microphones on the Glasses are activated and the following information is collected:</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Photos and video recordings</span>. You can use the Glasses to take photos and video recordings with audio and this content can be edited in the App. This content is stored on your Glasses, until it’s uploaded to your App. </p></li><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Metadata</span>. We collect metadata in or about the content, such as the date and time you created it, whether it’s a photo or a video recording, and technical information about your camera or other Glasses sensors related to the content. </p></li></ul></li><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Device information</span>: We collect "Essential Data," and, if you choose to share it, "Additional Data," about your Glasses and the App when you use Facebook View.</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Essential Data</span> is information needed to help make the Glasses and the App reliable, secure, and operating normally. For example, we collect information to see whether they’re working correctly, like when you’re pairing the Glasses with the App. We also collect information to make sure it’s you, like when you sign into the App with your Meta account or perform certain actions on the Glasses and App. In addition, similar to other devices or apps, when Facebook View crashes or malfunctions, a log is sent to Meta that includes information from the time of the crash event, such as the date and time of the crash and what features of the App you used immediately before the crash event.
                      </p></li><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Additional Data</span>  is information about how you use the Glasses and the App. We primarily use this information to improve the App and Glasses. For example, we collect information like the number of photos and videos you take, the method you use to share them, how long you spend taking videos, and their average length. If you do choose to share Additional Data, it may be combined with the Essential Data we collect. You can choose to share Additional Data during your initial setup, or change your choice at any time in Settings. <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="/help/ray-ban-stories/articles/legal-and-privacy-information/control-what-information-you-share-with-facebook-on-facebook-view/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_self">Learn more</a> about Additional Data and your choice to share it with Meta.
                      </p></li></ul></li></ul><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">When we collect Essential and Additional Data, we associate it with other information, like your User ID, Device ID, and information about your device model and operating system.</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Third-party services</span>: When a third-party service is used on the Glasses, like a music player, depending on how the service works, we may collect information about how you use it. This includes how often and for how long you use it, crash log information if it crashes, and an authorization token if it requires a log-in. Third-party services may share information with us when their service is used on the Glasses. To learn about how third-party services process your information, please refer to their terms and privacy policies.</p></li></ul><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">II. How do we use your information for Facebook View? </span></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">In addition to the purposes described in the Meta Privacy Policy under "<a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/privacy/policy/?section_id=2-HowDoWeUse" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">How do we use your information?</a>", we use the information we collect in the following ways:</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Provide our services</span>. We use Essential Data in accordance with the <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/privacy/policy/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">Meta Privacy Policy</a>. For example, we use this information to evaluate the usefulness of the features we are developing, which helps us create features you want. <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="/help/ray-ban-stories/articles/legal-and-privacy-information/control-what-information-you-share-with-facebook-on-facebook-view/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_self">Learn more</a> about Additional Data and your choice to share it with Meta.</p></li></ul><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">You can choose to communicate and share content on Facebook View using other <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/help/195227921252400?ref=dp" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">Meta Company Products</a>. How is your information shared with others for Facebook View? </span></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">We share information we collect when you use Facebook View as described in the Meta Privacy Policy under “<a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/privacy/policy/?section_id=3-HowIsYourInformation" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">How is your information shared on Meta Products or with Integrated Partners?</a>” and “<a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/privacy/policy/?section_id=4-HowDoWeShare" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">How do we share information with Partners, vendors, service providers and third parties?</a>” and as described in the following sections. We may also access, preserve, use and share your information as described in the Meta Privacy Policy under “<a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/privacy/policy/?section_id=10-HowDoWeRespond" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">How do we respond to legal requests, comply with applicable law and prevent harm?</a>”</p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">IV. How do we process information when you use our voice services for Facebook View?</span></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">This Section applies when our voice services, like voice assistant, are available on Facebook View and you enable them.</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">
                    When you use our voice services, we process information about your voice interactions to respond to your requests. Voice interactions are things you say when using our voice services, including when voice services are invoked by mistake, as well as any background sound that can be heard once voice services are enabled.  The information we process includes audio recordings and transcripts of your voice interactions, as well as data related to your voice interactions, like the hardware version of your Glasses and how long your interaction took.</p></li><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">
                    Depending on your preferences in Settings, we may also store and process information about your voice interactions to improve our voice services. For example, this information can help our voice services to better understand and respond more accurately to a wide range of speech patterns and phrases over time. You can manage voice storage to improve our voice services in your Settings.  When voice storage and processing for product improvement is turned on, we use machine learning and trained reviewers to process information about your voice interactions to improve, troubleshoot, and train our voice services. We share that information with third party vendors and service providers to improve our products. You can access and delete stored voice information in your Settings.</p></li><li class=""><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">
                    You can learn more about our voice services, including further details about what information we collect when you use our voice services and your choices over how we process that information, in the <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="/help/ray-ban-stories/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_self">Voice Services FAQ</a>.</p></li></ul><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">V. How do Meta and Luxottica work together?</span></p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Luxottica Group S.p.A. (“Luxottica”) is the manufacturer and distributor of the Glasses. Any information you provide to Luxottica in connection with your purchase of the Glasses is subject to Luxottica’s terms and policies. We exchange information with Luxottica to manage your customer service requests. For example, Luxottica shares with us your name, email address and information about the issue you are experiencing. Then we share with Luxottica information to help resolve the issue, such as steps to resolve a problem with your Meta account. We also exchange aggregated information and insights with Luxottica relating to marketing, usage, sales, and post-sale activities. Luxottica does not collect information directly from your use of the Glasses and the App.
